			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#x201C;Fiscal year 2020 brought us many unexpected challenges but </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">it </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">also</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> brought</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> many unexpected opportunities,&#x201D; said Garry Ridge, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">WD-40 Company&#x2019;s chairman and chief executive officer. </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#x201C;As a global business that </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">sells products</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> in </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">more than </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">176 countries</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> and territories</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> around the world, each of our </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">markets</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> &nbsp;w</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">ere</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> impacted differently by the COVID-19 pandemic and therefore our sales results var</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">ied</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> greatly between geographies. In geographies where retail operations remained open and where we were able to leverage our strong digital presence, we saw strong sales growth. However, in markets with strict movement restrictions in place or less developed e-commerce adoption, our sales were challenged.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#x201D;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> &nbsp; &nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 36pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xFEFF;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 36pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#x201C;An unexpected </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">developing trend</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> we experienced in the fourth quarter </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">was</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> an</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> increase</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> in</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> demand for products linked to renovation trends associated with the COVID-19 pandemic.&nbsp; </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">It seems </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">that the more time people spend isolated in their homes, the more time and money they spend making home improvements.&nbsp;&nbsp;We are calling this trend, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#x2018;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">isolation renovation</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#x2019;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-style:italic;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">and </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">in nearly all our direct markets we saw double-digit sales growth of WD-40 Multi-Use Product due to th</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">is</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> phenomenon.&#x201D;&nbsp;&nbsp; </font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">

		</p>
		<p><font size="1"> </font></p><div style="width:100%">

		<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:center;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">

			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"></font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"></font>

		</p>

		<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">

			&nbsp;

		</p>

</div><hr size="3" style="color:#999999" width="100%" align="center"></hr><p style="page-break-after:always">&nbsp;</p><div style="width:100%">

		</p>

			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;">&#xFEFF;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 36pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;">&#x201C;I also want to take this opportunity to thank our tribe for their commitment during these challenging times. Thank you for working hard to ensure that customer orders </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;">were</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;"> obtained, production lines </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;">were</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;"> functioning, orders </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;">were</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;"> fulfilled, and customers and end-users </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;">were</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;"> getting the products they need.&nbsp;&nbsp;2020 has been challenging but we have successfully been able to</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> stabilize, secure, and reset our business so that we will thrive in the future,&#x201D; concluded Ridge. </font>

		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">
			<p style="line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0.1pt 0pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">Net sales of maintenance products, which are considered the primary growth focus for the Company, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">increased </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">4</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;"> percent</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;"> in the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">fourth</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;"> quarter </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">when </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">compared to the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">prior year </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">fiscal quarter</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">.&nbsp; </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">This sales growth was primarily attributable to increased sales of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">WD-40 Multi-Use Product </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">and WD-40 BIKE </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">within the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Americas and EMEA</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> segment</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">s</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, which were partially offset by lower sales of WD-40 Multi-Use Product in the Asia-Pacific segment.&nbsp; </font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%; table-layout: fixed;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:18pt;"><p style="width:18pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt;">
			<p style="line-height:115%;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0.1pt 0pt;">
				<font style="margin:0.1pt 0pt;font-family:Symbol;line-height:115%;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;;"> &#xB7;</font>
			</p>
		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">
			<p style="line-height:115%;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0.1pt 0pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Net sales of homecare and cleaning products </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">increased by 15 percent </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">in the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">fourth</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> quarter </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">when </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">compared to the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">prior </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">year fiscal quarter</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">. &nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">We experienced a significant increase in sales of our homecare and cleaning products beginning in the third quarter of fiscal year 2020 due to increased demand for such products as a result of the COVID-19 pandemic. While each of our homecare and cleaning products have continued to generate positive </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">cash flows, we had experienced decreased or flat sales for many of these products in recent years prior to the COVID-19 pandemic.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>

			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">As previously announced, WD-40 Company&#x2019;s board of directors declared on </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">Monday</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">, October </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">5</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">, 20</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">20</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;"> a quarterly dividend of $0.6</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">7</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;"> per share payable October 3</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">0</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">, 20</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">20</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;"> to stockholders of record at the close of business on October 1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">6</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">, 20</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">20</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">.</font>

			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">On June 19, 2018, the Company&#x2019;s Board of Directors approved a share buy-back plan. Under the plan, which became effective on September 1, 2018</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">, and remained in effect through August 31, 2020</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">, the Company </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">wa</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">s authorized to acquire up to $75.0 million of its outstanding shares. During the period from September 1, 2018 through August 31, 20</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">20</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">, the Company repurchased </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">268,538</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;"> shares at a total cost of $</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">46.4</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;"> million under this $75.0 million plan.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">On April 8, 2020, the Company elected to suspend repurchases under this share buy-back plan which </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">subsequently </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">expired on August 31, 2020. The Company </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">suspended repurchases</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> in order to preserve cash while it continued to monitor the impacts of the COVID-19 pandemic. Therefore, no repurchase transactions were made between April 8, 2020 and August 31, 2020.</font>

			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">About WD-40 Company</font>

The Company </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">owns</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> a wide range of</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> maintenance</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> products and</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">homecare and cleaning products under the following well-known brands: WD-40&#xAE;, 3-IN-ONE&#xAE;, GT85&#xAE;, X-14&#xAE;, 2000 Flushes&#xAE;, Carpet Fresh&#xAE;, no vac&#xAE;, Spot Shot&#xAE;, 1001&#xAE;,&nbsp;Lava&#xAE;</font><font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">and Solvol&#xAE;. &nbsp;</font>
